```python
import pandas as pd
from sklearn.externals import joblib

model = joblib.load('clinical_notes_model')

df = pd.read_csv(""../data/vaxx_data.csv"")
df['VAERS_ID'] = df.apply(lambda row: model.predict(row), axis=1)
```
